        "confirmed_ts": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",
        "contracts": 123,
        "created_ts": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",
        "creator_id": "<string>",
        "creator_order_id": "<string>",
        "creator_user_id": "<string>",
        "executed_ts": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",
        "id": "<string>",
        "market_ticker": "<string>",
        "no_bid": 123,

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/communications/get-quote#parameter-quote-id)

quote\_id

string

required

Quote ID

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Create Quote](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/communications/create-quote)
[Delete Quote](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/communications/delete-quote)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

              {\
                "close_time": "<string>",\
                "open_time": "<string>"\
              }\
            ],\

              {\
                "close_time": "<string>",\

            ],\

        "product_metadata": {
          "key": {}
        },
        "settlement_sources": [\
          "<any>"\
        ],
        "tags": [\
          "<string>"\
        ],
        "ticker": "<string>",
        "title": "<string>"
      }
    }

string

required

          "title": "<string>"\
        }\
      ]

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-events#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Parameter to specify the number of results per page. Defaults to 100. Maximum value is 200.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-events#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

Parameter to specify the pagination cursor. Use the cursor value returned from the previous response to get the next page of results. Leave empty for the first page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-events#parameter-with-nested-markets)

with\_nested\_markets

boolean

Parameter to specify if nested markets should be included in the response. When true, each event will include a 'markets' field containing a list of Market objects associated with that event.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-events#parameter-status)

status

string

Filter by event status. Possible values: 'open', 'closed', 'settled'. Leave empty to return events with any status.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-events#parameter-series-ticker)

series\_ticker

string

Filter events by series ticker. Returns only events belonging to the specified series.

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Delete RFQ](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/communications/delete-rfq)
[Get Event](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-event)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

      "cursor": "<string>",
      "markets": [\
        {\
          "ticker": "<string>",\
          "event_ticker": "<string>",\
          "market_type": "<string>",\
          "title": "<string>",\
          "subtitle": "<string>",\
          "yes_sub_title": "<string>",\
          "no_sub_title": "<string>",\
          "open_time": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "close_time": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "expiration_time": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "latest_expiration_time": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "settlement_timer_seconds": 123,\
          "status": "<string>",\
          "response_price_units": "<string>",\
          "notional_value": 123,\
          "tick_size": 123,\
          "yes_bid": 123,\
          "yes_ask": 123,\
          "no_bid": 123,\
          "no_ask": 123,\
          "last_price": 123,\
          "previous_yes_bid": 123,\
          "previous_yes_ask": 123,\
          "previous_price": 123,\
          "volume": 123,\
          "volume_24h": 123,\
          "liquidity": 123,\
          "open_interest": 123,\
          "result": "<string>",\
          "can_close_early": true,\
          "expiration_value": "<string>",\
          "category": "<string>",\
          "risk_limit_cents": 123,\
          "rules_primary": "<string>",\
          "rules_secondary": "<string>",\
          "settlement_value": 123,\
          "settlement_value_dollars": "<string>"\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Number of results per page. Defaults to 100. Maximum value is 1000.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

Pagination cursor. Use the cursor value returned from the previous response to get the next page of results. Leave empty for the first page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-event-ticker)

event\_ticker

string

Filter markets by event ticker. Returns only markets belonging to the specified event.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-series-ticker)

series\_ticker

string

Filter markets by series ticker. Returns only markets belonging to events in the specified series.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-max-close-ts)

max\_close\_ts

integer

Filter markets that close before this Unix timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-min-close-ts)

min\_close\_ts

integer

Filter markets that close after this Unix timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-status)

status

string

Filter by market status. Comma-separated list. Possible values: 'unopened', 'open', 'closed', 'settled'. Leave empty to return markets with any status.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets#parameter-tickers)

tickers

string

Filter by specific market tickers. Comma-separated list of market tickers to retrieve.

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Get Event Metadata](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-event-metadata)
[Get Trades](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market-candlesticks#parameter-series-ticker)

series\_ticker

string

required

Series ticker - the series that contains the target market

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market-candlesticks#parameter-ticker)

ticker

string

required

Market ticker - unique identifier for the specific market

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market-candlesticks#parameter-start-ts)

start\_ts

integer

required

Start timestamp (Unix timestamp). Candlesticks will include those ending on or after this time.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market-candlesticks#parameter-end-ts)

end\_ts

integer

required

End timestamp (Unix timestamp). Candlesticks will include those ending on or before this time.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market-candlesticks#parameter-period-interval)

period\_interval

integer

required

Time period length of each candlestick in minutes. Valid values: 1 (1 minute), 60 (1 hour), 1440 (1 day).

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Get Series](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-series)
[Get Exchange Announcements](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/get-exchange-announcements)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

integer

required

/

trades

Try it

Get Trades

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.elections.kalshi.com/trade-api/v2/markets/trades

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "cursor": "<string>",
      "trades": [\
        {\
          "count": 123,\
          "created_time": "<any>",\
          "no_price": 123,\
          "taker_side": "yes",\
          "ticker": "<string>",\
          "trade_id": "<string>",\
          "yes_price": 123\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Number of results per page. Defaults to 100. Maximum value is 1000.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

Pagination cursor. Use the cursor value returned from the previous response to get the next page of results. Leave empty for the first page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades#parameter-ticker)

ticker

string

Filter trades by market ticker. Returns only trades for the specified market.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades#parameter-min-ts)

min\_ts

integer

Filter trades that occurred after this Unix timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-trades#parameter-max-ts)

max\_ts

integer

Filter trades that occurred before this Unix timestamp.

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Get Markets](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-markets)
[Get Market](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/market/get-market)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Get Fills

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.elections.kalshi.com/trade-api/v2/portfolio/fills

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "cursor": "<string>",
      "fills": [\
        {\
          "action": "buy",\
          "count": 123,\
          "created_time": "<any>",\
          "is_taker": true,\
          "no_price": 123,\
          "no_price_fixed": [\
            123\
          ],\
          "order_id": "<string>",\
          "side": "yes",\

          "trade_id": "<string>",\

            123\
          ]\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-ticker)

ticker

string

Restricts the response to trades in a specific market.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-order-id)

order\_id

string

Restricts the response to trades related to a specific order.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-min-ts)

min\_ts

integer

Restricts the response to trades after a timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-max-ts)

max\_ts

integer

Restricts the response to trades before a timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Parameter to specify the number of results per page. Defaults to 100.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

The Cursor represents a pointer to the next page of records in the pagination. Use the value returned from the previous response to get the next page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-fills#parameter-use-dollars)

use\_dollars

boolean

Whether to return prices in centi-cent format (0.0001) instead of cent format (0.01).

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Get Balance](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-balance)
[Get Order Groups](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-order-groups)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

The Cursor represents a pointer to the next page of records in the pagination. Use the value returned from the previous response to get the next page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Parameter to specify the number of results per page. Defaults to 100.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-count-filter)

count\_filter

string

Restricts the positions to those with any of following fields with non-zero values, as a comma separated list. The following values are accepted: position, total\_traded, resting\_order\_count

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-settlement-status)

settlement\_status

string

Settlement status of the markets to return. Defaults to unsettled.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-ticker)

ticker

string

Ticker of desired positions.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-positions#parameter-event-ticker)

event\_ticker

string

Event ticker of desired positions.

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Get Queue Position for Order](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-queue-position-for-order)
[Get Settlements](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-settlements)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-ticker)

ticker

string

Restricts the response to orders in a single market.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-event-ticker)

event\_ticker

string

Restricts the response to orders in a single event.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-min-ts)

min\_ts

integer

Restricts the response to orders after a timestamp, formatted as a Unix Timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-max-ts)

max\_ts

integer

Restricts the response to orders before a timestamp, formatted as a Unix Timestamp.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-status)

status

string

Restricts the response to orders that have a certain status: resting, canceled, or executed.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

The Cursor represents a pointer to the next page of records in the pagination. Use the value returned from the previous response to get the next page.

[​](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/get-orders#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Parameter to specify the number of results per page. Defaults to 100.

#### Response

200 - application/json

The response is of type `object`.

[Reset Order Group](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/reset-order-group)
[Create Order](https://docs.kalshi.com/api-reference/portfolio/create-order)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.
